 ham aapako bataa rahe hai kidonon shabdon main kya antar haior unka kya matlab he?1) Grocery Store (american english) or Super Market (british english)- Grocery Store main kichan ke saare jaruri saamaan, sabji aadi chijen milti hai
 The term Super Market is also used for the Grocery Store
 2)restaurant (american english) or Hotel (british english)-yues main hotelka matlab us jagah se he jahaan aap raat bhar rukate hai
 3) Cross Walk (american English) and Zebra Crossing (british English) - a route designed to cross the road at a traffic light
 4) Traffic Lights (american english) or Traffic Signal (british english)- yues main trephic signal ke liye log trephic lits yaa lits shabdon kaa prayog karte hai
 5) Soda (american English) and Cold Drink (british English) - The words Soda are used for things like Coke, Pepsi etc
 6) Pills (american english) or Tablets (british english)- yues main agar aap biimaar hai to aap Pills lete hai
 Pills are taken for cold, allergies
 7) Clippers (american english) or Nail Cutter (british english)- yues main nakhun Clippers se kaate jate hai
 8) Pants (american English) and Trousers (british English) - called pants in the US and trousers in the UK
 9) Sneakers (american english) or Tennis Shoe / Sports Shoe (british english)- yues main running shoej ke liye snikers kaa prayog hota he
 10) Eraser (american English) and Rubber (british English) - Use eraser in the US to erase pencil handwriting

 1
 In the UAE, a person cannot live with a woman without marriage

 2

 3

 Somebody is hanged there in 3 ways

 There have also been many questions on the manner in which the death penalty has been awarded in the United Arab Emirates
 4
 There is a ban on eating and drinking in public transport in the United Arab Emirates

 5

 In his next over, Naren looted 10 runs
 antim 12 gendon main super kings ko 17 ran banane the
 Jadeja and Dwayne Bravo teamed up with this over by Kallis to seal his team's victory
 ant main jadeja ne chakke ke saath apni team ko jeet dilaa di
 Earlier, Knight Riders came out to bat first after winning the toss and scored 119 runs losing nine wickets in the prescribed 20 overs
 nite rides kii ore se yusuf pathan or captain gautam gambhir ne 25-25 ranon kii pari kheli
 Apart from this, Devvrat Das contributed 19 runs
 super kings kii ore se rabindra jadeja ne teen or ravichandran aswin ne do safaltaaen hasil kii
 The Knight Riders got off to a good start by Yusuf Pathan and captain Gautam Gambhir, who started the innings in place of Manvinder Bisla
 donon ne pehle paanch over main 46 ran jode
 Pathan, who could not impress with the bat so far, made some good shots
 46 ranon ke kul yoga par maaikel hasi ne seemaa rekha par gambhir kaa shandaar kaich lapakkar unhen pavilion kii raah dikhaai
 Gambhir hit five fours in 19 balls
 gambhir ke out hone par ballebaaji karne aae jacks kallis bagaiyr khaataa khole ran out ho gaye
 He was runout by Badrinath
 50 ranon ke kul yoga par is toornament main shandaar form main chal rahe ian morgan do ran banaakar chalate bane
 Pathan, batting brilliantly on the sum of 54 runs, was run out to take the second run
 pathan ne 22 gendon kaa saamana kiya
 During this, he also hit four fours
 acchhee shuruyaat ke baavjood nite rides ne mahaj 10 ranon ke bheetar apane chaar sheersh ballebaajon ke wicket ganvaae
 The comments paanchaven wicket ke liye manoj tiwari or das ne apni team ke liye 27 ranon kii ahm saajhedaari kii
 But Das fell lbw to Ravichandran Ashwin for a total of 82 runs
 das ne 15 gendon kaa saamana kiya or do chakke jade
 After this, the Knight Riders' innings was once again faltered
 nite rides ne 100 ranon andar hi apane aath ballebaaj ganvaa die
 In the end, Sunil Narine hit two sixes in an over from Ravindra Jadeja to take his team's score to a respectable position, but he was dismissed by 13 runs
 super kings kii ore maaikel hasi ne sabase zyada 40 ranon kii pari kheli
 Apart from this, Ravindra Jadeja hit a quick 36-run knock
 jadeja ne 14 gendon kaa saamana karte hue teen chakke or teen chauke jade
 The Super Kings got off to a poor start
 captain mahendra singh ne sabhi ko chaunkaate hue maaikel hasi ke saath ravichandran aswin (11) ko pari kii shuruyaat karne ke liye bheja
 But Ashwin could not justify the captain's decision
 24 ranon ke kul yoga par aswin sunil naren kaa shikaar bane
 Murali Vijay (02), who came out to bat after Ashwin, was lbw for a total of 31 runs
 40 ranon ke kul yoga par super kings ko teesraa jhatka laga
 Suresh Raina returned to the pavilion after scoring seven runs
 iske baad 54 ranon ke kul yoga par mahendra singh dhoni ke rup main super kings ko chauthaa jhatka laga
 The Super Kings lost successive wickets, but Hussey held one end firmly
 71 ranon ke kul yoga par subramanyam badrinaath 6 ran banaakar chalate bane
 It was the fifth wicket of the Super Kings
 hasi ke rup main super kings kaa chatha wicket 89 ran par gira

 lakshya kaa peechha karne utari super kings kii shuruyaat kharaab rahi
 Skipper Mahendra Singh shocked everyone, sending Ravichandran Ashwin (11) with Michael Hussey to start the innings
 lekin aswin captain ke faisle ko sahi sabit nahin kar sake
 Ashwin became the victim of Sunil Narine with a total of 24 runs
 aswin ke out hone par ballebaaji karne aae murali vijay (02) 31 ranon ke kul yoga par pagabaadha hue
 The Super Kings got their third blow at a total of 40 runs
 suresh raina saat ran banaakar pavilion laut gaye
 After this, Super Kings got the fourth blow as Mahendra Singh Dhoni on a total of 54 runs
 super kings ne lagaataar wicket ganvaae, lekin hasi ne ek chor ko majbootee se thame rakhaa
 Subramanian Badrinath went on to score 6 runs at a total of 71 runs
 yah super kings kaa paanchavaa wicket tha
 The sixth wicket of Super Kings as Hussey fell to 89 runs
 hasi ne 51 gendon kaa saamana kiya or do chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 The Super Kings had to score 40 runs to win the final four overs, after which Jadeja added 13 runs in Balaji's over in the 17th over
 iske agle over main naren 10 ran lutaae
 The Super Kings were to score 17 runs in the final 12 balls
 jadeja or or dwen braavo ne milakar kallis dwaara kiye gaye is over 13 ran thok kar apni team kii jeet pakki kar di
 In the end, Jadeja gave his team the victory with a six
 isse pehle, toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karne utari nite rides ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main nau wicket khokar 119 ran banaae
 For the Knight Riders, Yusuf Pathan and captain Gautam Gambhir scored 25-25 runs
 iske alaava devvrat das ne 19 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Ravindra Jadeja from Super Kings scored three and Ravichandran Ashwin had two successes
 nite rides ko manvinder bislaa kii jagah pari kii shuruyaat karne aae yusuf pathan or captain gautam gambhir ne behatar shuruyaat di
 Both added 46 runs in the first five overs
 ab tak balle se prabhavit nahin kar sake pathan ne kuch achche shots lagaae
 On the total of 46 runs, Michael Hussey caught Gambhir's brilliant catch at the boundary line and showed him the path of the pavilion
 gambhir ne 19 gendon main paanch chauke jade
 Jacques Kallis, who came to bat on Gambhir's dismissal, was run out without opening an account
 unhen badrinaath ne ranout kiya
 Ian Morgan, who was in excellent form in this tournament at a total of 50 runs, went on to score two runs
 54 ranon ke yoga par badhiya ballebaaji kar rahe pathan doosraa ran lene ke chakkar main ran out ho gaye
 Pathan faced 22 balls
 is dauraan unhone chaar chauke bhi jade

 tippaniyan Manoj Tiwari and Das made a vital partnership of 27 runs for their team for the fifth wicket
 lekin das 82 ranon ke kul yoga par ravichandran aswin kii gend par pagabaadha ho gaye

 iske baad ek baar phir se nite rides kii pari ladkadaa gai
